📦 Distributed Execution Architecture
1. Distributed Execution Engine (DxEE)

Description:
A distributed execution engine that allows the framework to run across multiple nodes.

Functions:

    Task distribution
    Load balancing
    Node management
    Resource allocation

Tools Used:

    Docker
    Kubernetes
    Kali Linux Tools
    Python
    Bash
    Brew
    Pipx

2. Node Management Module (NMM)

Description:
A module that manages the nodes in the distributed execution environment.

Functions:

    Node discovery
    Node status monitoring
    Node health checking
    Node resource allocation

Tools Used:

    Docker
    Kubernetes
    Python
    Bash
    Brew
    Pipx

3. Load Balancing Module (LBM)

Description:
A module that balances the load across the nodes.

Functions:

    Task distribution
    Load balancing
    Resource allocation
    Node status monitoring

Tools Used:

    Docker
    Kubernetes
    Python
    Bash
    Brew
    Pipx

📌 Framework Upgrade and Expansion Assessment
✅ Upgrade Summary

    Framework Type: Military-Grade Penetration Testing and Information Security Framework
    Tool Integration: All Kali Linux tools, Python-based tools, Bash scripts, Docker, Kubernetes, etc.
    Intelligence Loops: 5+ intelligent loops for threat intelligence, attack surface management, exploitation, reconnaissance, and automation
    Pipelines: 5+ pipelines for reconnaissance, exploitation, attack surface management, intelligence, and automation
    Modules: 5+ modules for reconnaissance, exploitation, attack surface management, intelligence, and automation
    Workflows: 5+ workflows for reconnaissance, exploitation, attack surface management, intelligence, and automation
    Distributed Execution: Distributed execution engine and node management module for large-scale operations

🚀 Future Expansion Options

    Add more intelligent loops for AI-based threat prediction and risk scoring
    Integrate machine learning models for attack pattern recognition
    Add support for cloud-based execution (e.g., AWS, Azure, GCP)
    Add support for container orchestration (e.g., Kubernetes, Docker Swarm)
    Add support for multi-cloud environments
    Add support for real-time data processing and analytics
    Add support for visualization and reporting (e.g., Grafana, Kibana, etc.)
    Add support for multi-language execution (e.g., Python, Java, C++, etc.)
    Add support for multi-platform execution (e.g., Windows, Linux, macOS, etc.)
    Add support for multi-team collaboration (e.g., Slack, Discord, etc.)
    Add support for multi-client environments (e.g., Red Team, Blue Team, etc.)

🧾 Conclusion

The R4NG3R-V2 framework has been upgraded to a massively distributed, autonomous, and fully integrated system that combines advanced pipelines, intelligent loops, modular workflows, and multi-tool integration. This version is designed to be a military-grade penetration testing and information security framework that can be used for red teaming, blue teaming, advanced threat simulation, and full-scale cyber warfare.

This upgrade ensures that the framework is complete, detailed, and advanced, and is ready for use in any penetration testing or information security scenario.

SECTION 3: ADVANCED PIPELINES (60+ PIPELINES)
Pipeline Standard Structure
yaml
pipeline:
  name: pipeline_name
  input: [input_types]
  stages:
    - stage_name:
        tools: [tool_list]
        module: module_name
        output_format: [formats]
        recursive_pivot: true/false
        ai_correlation: true/false
  reporting:
    formats: [JSON, CSV, XLSX, PDF, HTML, MTGL]
    dashboard: true/false
    next_steps: [action_list]

SECTION 2: CORE FRAMEWORK MODULES
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

### 2.1: BASE MODULE CLASS (core_v3/base_module.py)

```python
import logging
import asyncio
import time
from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
from enum import Enum
from typing import Dict, Any, List, Optional
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from datetime import datetime

class ModuleType(Enum):
    """Module execution types"""
    RECONNAISSANCE = "reconnaissance"
    OSINT = "osint"
    VULNERABILITY = "vulnerability"
    EXPLOITATION = "exploitation"
    POST_EXPLOIT = "post_exploitation"
    REPORTING = "reporting"
    AUTOMATION = "automation"

class ModuleStatus(Enum):
    """Module execution status"""
    PENDING = "pending"
    RUNNING = "running"
    SUCCESS = "success"
    FAILED = "failed"
    PARTIAL = "partial"
    TIMEOUT = "timeout"

@dataclass
class ModuleResult:
    """Standard result format for all modules"""
    module_name: str
    status: ModuleStatus
    start_time: str
    end_time: str
    duration: float
    output: Dict[str, Any]
    errors: List[str]
    warnings: List[str]
    relationships: List[Dict[str, Any]]
    
    def to_dict(self):
        return asdict(self)

class BaseModule(ABC):
    """
    Base class for all R4NG3R-V3 modules.
    Provides standardized interface, error handling, and logging.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.name = config.get('name', 'UnnamedModule')
        self.module_type = config.get('type', ModuleType.RECONNAISSANCE)
        self.timeout = config.get('timeout', 300)
        self.max_retries = config.get('max_retries', 3)
        self.retry_delay = config.get('retry_delay', 5)
        self.continue_on_error = config.get('continue_on_error', True)
        self.fallback_tools = config.get('fallback_tools', [])
        
        self.start_time = None
        self.end_time = None
        self.logger = self._setup_logger()
        self.result = None
    
    def _setup_logger(self) -> logging.Logger:
        """Setup module-specific logger"""
        logger = logging.getLogger(f"r4ng3r.{self.name}")
        handler = logging.FileHandler(f"logs/{self.name}.log")
        formatter = logging.Formatter(
            '%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
        )
        handler.setFormatter(formatter)
        logger.addHandler(handler)
        logger.setLevel(logging.INFO)
        return logger
    
    @abstractmethod
    def execute(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Execute the module.
        Must be implemented by subclasses.
        """
        pass
    
    @abstractmethod
    def validate_input(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        """
        Validate input data schema.
        Must be implemented by subclasses.
        """
        pass
    
    async def execute_async(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> ModuleResult:
        """
        Asynchronous module execution with error handling
        """
        self.start_time = datetime.now()
        errors = []
        warnings = []
        
        try:
            # Validate input
            if not self.validate_input(input_data):
                raise ValueError("Invalid input data")
            
            # Attempt execution with retries
            output = None
            for attempt in range(self.max_retries):
                try:
                    self.logger.info(f"Execution attempt {attempt + 1}/{self.max_retries}")
                    output = await asyncio.wait_for(
                        asyncio.to_thread(self.execute, input_data),
                        timeout=self.timeout
                    )
                    break
                except asyncio.TimeoutError:
                    errors.append(f"Timeout on attempt {attempt + 1}")
                    if attempt < self.max_retries - 1:
                        await asyncio.sleep(self.retry_delay)
                except Exception as e:
                    errors.append(f"Attempt {attempt + 1} failed: {str(e)}")
                    if attempt < self.max_retries - 1:
                        await asyncio.sleep(self.retry_delay)
            
            if output is None and not self.continue_on_error:
                raise Exception("Module execution failed and continue_on_error=False")
            
            # Extract relationships if present
            relationships = output.get('relationships', []) if output else []
            
            self.end_time = datetime.now()
            duration = (self.end_time - self.start_time).total_seconds()
            
            status = ModuleStatus.SUCCESS if output else ModuleStatus.PARTIAL
            
            self.result = ModuleResult(
                module_name=self.name,
                status=status,
                start_time=self.start_time.isoformat(),
                end_time=self.end_time.isoformat(),
                duration=duration,
                output=output or {},
                errors=errors,
                warnings=warnings,
                relationships=relationships
            )
            
            self.logger.info(f"Module execution completed with status: {status.value}")
            return self.result
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.end_time = datetime.now()
            duration = (self.end_time - self.start_time).total_seconds()
            
            self.logger.error(f"Module execution failed: {str(e)}")
            
            self.result = ModuleResult(
                module_name=self.name,
                status=ModuleStatus.FAILED,
                start_time=self.start_time.isoformat(),
                end_time=self.end_time.isoformat(),
                duration=duration,
                output={},
                errors=[str(e)],
                warnings=warnings,
                relationships=[]
            )
            
            return self.result
    
    def run(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> ModuleResult:
        """Synchronous execution wrapper"""
        return asyncio.run(self.execute_async(input_data))
```

### 2.2: TOOL REGISTRY (core_v3/tool_registry.py)

```python
import os
import json
import importlib.util
from typing import Dict, Type, Optional, List
from pathlib import Path
import logging

class ToolRegistry:
    """
    Central registry for tool discovery, loading, and management.
    Supports dynamic loading from filesystem and Git repositories.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, tools_path: str = 'tools_v3'):
        self.tools: Dict[str, Type] = {}
        self.tools_path = Path(tools_path)
        self.logger = logging.getLogger("r4ng3r.ToolRegistry")
        self.tool_metadata: Dict[str, Dict] = {}
    
    def auto_discover_tools(self) -> int:
        """
        Automatically discover and load all tool modules.
        Returns count of discovered tools.
        """
        discovered_count = 0
        
        for category_dir in self.tools_path.iterdir():
            if not category_dir.is_dir():
                continue
            
            for tool_file in category_dir.glob('*_tool.py'):
                try:
                    tool_name = tool_file.stem.replace('_tool', '')
                    tool_class = self._load_tool_module(tool_file)
                    
                    if tool_class:
                        self.register(tool_name, tool_class)
                        discovered_count += 1
                        self.logger.info(f"Discovered tool: {tool_name}")
                
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.warning(f"Failed to load {tool_file}: {str(e)}")
        
        self.logger.info(f"Discovered {discovered_count} tools")
        return discovered_count
    
    def _load_tool_module(self, file_path: Path) -> Optional[Type]:
        """Load a tool module from file"""
        try:
            spec = importlib.util.spec_from_file_location(
                file_path.stem,
                file_path
            )
            module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
            spec.loader.exec_module(module)
            
            # Find the main tool class (typically named Tool or *Tool)
            for attr_name in dir(module):
                attr = getattr(module, attr_name)
                if isinstance(attr, type) and 'Tool' in attr_name:
                    return attr
            
            return None
        
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Failed to load {file_path}: {str(e)}")
            return None
    
    def register(self, tool_name: str, tool_class: Type, metadata: Dict = None) -> None:
        """Register a tool in the registry"""
        if tool_name in self.tools:
            self.logger.warning(f"Tool {tool_name} already registered, updating")
        
        self.tools[tool_name] = tool_class
        self.tool_metadata[tool_name] = metadata or {}
        self.logger.info(f"Tool registered: {tool_name}")
    
    def get_tool(self, tool_name: str) -> Optional[Type]:
        """Retrieve a tool class by name"""
        return self.tools.get(tool_name)
    
    def get_tools_by_domain(self, domain: str) -> Dict[str, Type]:
        """Get all tools in a specific domain (reconnaissance, osint, etc.)"""
        return {
            name: tool for name, tool in self.tools.items()
            if self.tool_metadata.get(name, {}).get('domain') == domain
        }
    
    def list_tools(self) -> List[str]:
        """List all registered tools"""
        return list(self.tools.keys())
    
    def get_tool_info(self, tool_name: str) -> Dict:
        """Get metadata about a tool"""
        return {
            'name': tool_name,
            'class': self.tools.get(tool_name).__name__ if tool_name in self.tools else None,
            'metadata': self.tool_metadata.get(tool_name, {})
        }
    
    def export_registry(self, filepath: str) -> None:
        """Export registry to JSON file"""
        export_data = {
            name: {
                'class': tool.__name__,
                'metadata': self.tool_metadata.get(name, {})
            }
            for name, tool in self.tools.items()
        }
        
        with open(filepath, 'w') as f:
            json.dump(export_data, f, indent=2)
        
        self.logger.info(f"Registry exported to {filepath}")
```

### 2.3: PIPELINE ENGINE (core_v3/pipeline_engine.py)

```python
import yaml
import logging
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional
from datetime import datetime
from pathlib import Path
from concurrent.futures import ThreadPoolExecutor, as_completed
import json
import asyncio

class PipelineStage:
    """Represents a single stage in a pipeline"""
    
    def __init__(self, name: str, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.name = name
        self.tools = config.get('tools', [])
        self.parallel = config.get('parallel', False)
        self.timeout = config.get('timeout', 3600)
        self.fallback_tools = config.get('fallback_tools', [])
        self.continue_on_error = config.get('continue_on_error', True)
        self.transformations = config.get('transformations', [])
        self.outputs = config.get('outputs', [])

class PipelineEngine:
    """
    Main pipeline execution engine.
    Handles loading, executing, and monitoring pipelines.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, registry, pipelines_path: str = 'pipelines_v3'):
        self.registry = registry
        self.pipelines_path = Path(pipelines_path)
        self.logger = logging.getLogger("r4ng3r.PipelineEngine")
        self.pipelines: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}
        self.execution_history: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
    
    def load_pipeline(self, pipeline_name: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Load a pipeline definition from YAML file"""
        pipeline_file = self.pipelines_path / f"{pipeline_name}.yaml"
        
        if not pipeline_file.exists():
            self.logger.error(f"Pipeline file not found: {pipeline_file}")
            return None
        
        try:
            with open(pipeline_file, 'r') as f:
                pipeline_config = yaml.safe_load(f)
                self.pipelines[pipeline_name] = pipeline_config
                self.logger.info(f"Loaded pipeline: {pipeline_name}")
                return pipeline_config
        
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error loading pipeline: {str(e)}")
            return None
    
    async def execute_pipeline(self, pipeline_name: str, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Execute a complete pipeline with error handling and fallbacks.
        """
        pipeline = self.load_pipeline(pipeline_name)
        if not pipeline:
            return {"status": "error", "message": f"Pipeline {pipeline_name} not found"}
        
        execution_result = {
            'pipeline': pipeline_name,
            'start_time': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'stages': [],
            'status': 'running',
            'errors': [],
            'warnings': [],
            'relationships': []
        }
        
        try:
            stages = pipeline.get('stages', [])
            current_data = input_data
            
            for stage_config in stages:
                stage_name = stage_config.get('name', 'unnamed')
                stage_result = await self._execute_stage(stage_config, current_data)
                
                if stage_result.get('status') == 'error' and not stage_config.get('continue_on_error', True):
                    execution_result['status'] = 'failed'
                    execution_result['errors'].append(stage_result.get('error', 'Unknown error'))
                    break
                
                execution_result['stages'].append({
                    'name': stage_name,
                    'result': stage_result
                })
                
                # Extract relationships for graph integration
                if 'relationships' in stage_result:
                    execution_result['relationships'].extend(stage_result['relationships'])
                
                current_data = stage_result.get('output', current_data)
            
            execution_result['status'] = 'completed'
            execution_result['end_time'] = datetime.now().isoformat()
            execution_result['final_output'] = current_data
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Pipeline execution error: {str(e)}")
            execution_result['status'] = 'failed'
            execution_result['errors'].append(str(e))
        
        self.execution_history.append(execution_result)
        return execution_result
    
    async def _execute_stage(self, stage_config: Dict[str, Any], input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Execute a single pipeline stage with parallel/sequential tools"""
        stage_name = stage_config.get('name', 'unnamed')
        tools = stage_config.get('tools', [])
        parallel = stage_config.get('parallel', False)
        
        try:
            if parallel:
                results = await self._execute_parallel(tools, input_data)
            else:
                results = await self._execute_sequential(tools, input_data)
            
            # Aggregate relationships
            relationships = []
            for result in results:
                if isinstance(result.get('result'), dict):
                    relationships.extend(result.get('result', {}).get('relationships', []))
            
            return {
                'status': 'completed',
                'stage': stage_name,
                'tool_results': results,
                'output': {'results': results, 'input': input_data},
                'relationships': relationships
            }
        
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Stage execution error: {str(e)}")
            return {'status': 'error', 'error': str(e)}
    
    async def _execute_sequential(self, tools: List[str], input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Execute tools sequentially"""
        results = []
        
        for tool_name in tools:
            try:
                tool_class = self.registry.get_tool(tool_name)
                if not tool_class:
                    self.logger.warning(f"Tool not found: {tool_name}")
                    continue
                
                tool_instance = tool_class({'name': tool_name})
                result = await tool_instance.execute_async(input_data)
                results.append({'tool': tool_name, 'result': result.to_dict()})
            
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Tool {tool_name} execution error: {str(e)}")
                results.append({'tool': tool_name, 'error': str(e)})
        
        return results
    
    async def _execute_parallel(self, tools: List[str], input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """Execute tools in parallel"""
        tasks = []
        
        for tool_name in tools:
            tool_class = self.registry.get_tool(tool_name)
            if tool_class:
                tool_instance = tool_class({'name': tool_name})
                tasks.append((tool_name, tool_instance.execute_async(input_data)))
        
        results = []
        for tool_name, task in tasks:
            try:
                result = await task
                results.append({'tool': tool_name, 'result': result.to_dict()})
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Parallel tool {tool_name} failed: {str(e)}")
                results.append({'tool': tool_name, 'error': str(e)})
        
        return results
```

#### Tool 1: Amass Wrapper (tools_v3/reconnaissance/amass_tool.py)
```python
import subprocess
import json
import os
from typing import Dict, Any, List
from core_v3.base_module import BaseModule, ModuleType

class AmassTool(BaseModule):
    """
    OWASP Amass - Network mapper for DNS enumeration and network intelligence
    Modes: passive, active, brute force
    """
    
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        super().__init__(config)
        self.module_type = ModuleType.RECONNAISSANCE
        self.api_keys = config.get('api_keys', {})
        self.mode = config.get('mode', 'passive')
    
    def validate_input(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        required_fields = ['domain']
        return all(field in input_data for field in required_fields)
    
    def execute(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        domain = input_data.get('domain')
        output_file = f"/tmp/amass_{domain}.json"
        
        try:
            # Build Amass command
            cmd = ['amass', 'enum', '-d', domain, '-json', output_file]
            
            if self.mode == 'active':
                cmd.append('-active')
            
            if self.mode == 'brute':
                cmd.extend(['-brute'])
            
            # Add API keys if configured
            if self.api_keys.get('shodan'):
                os.environ['SHODAN_API_KEY'] = self.api_keys['shodan']
            
            self.logger.info(f"Running Amass on domain: {domain}")
            result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=self.timeout)
            
            if result.returncode != 0:
                self.logger.error(f"Amass failed: {result.stderr}")
                return {'subdomains': [], 'error': result.stderr}
            
            # Parse output
            subdomains = []
            relationships = []
            
            if os.path.exists(output_file):
                with open(output_file, 'r') as f:
                    for line in f:
                        try:
                            data = json.loads(line)
                            subdomain = data.get('name')
                            if subdomain:
                                subdomains.append(subdomain)
                                relationships.append({
                                    'source': domain,
                                    'target': subdomain,
                                    'relationship_type': 'dns_record'
                                })
                        except:
                            pass
            
            return {
                'subdomains': subdomains,
                'count': len(subdomains),
                'relationships': relationships
            }
        
        except subprocess.TimeoutExpired:
            self.logger.error(f"Amass timeout for domain {domain}")
            return {'error': 'timeout'}
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Amass execution failed: {str(e)}")
            return {'error': str(e)}
```

#### Tool 2: SpiderFoot Wrapper (tools_v3/reconnaissance/spiderfoot_tool.py)
```python
import subprocess
import json
from typing import Dict, Any
from core_v3.base_module import BaseModule, ModuleType

class SpiderfootTool(BaseModule):
    """
    SpiderFoot - Automated OSINT framework with 200+ modules
    """
    
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        super().__init__(config)
        self.module_type = ModuleType.OSINT
        self.spiderfoot_path = config.get('spiderfoot_path', '/opt/spiderfoot')
    
    def validate_input(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> bool:
        required_fields = ['target']
        return all(field in input_data for field in required_fields)
    
    def execute(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        target = input_data.get('target')
        
        try:
            cmd = [
                'python3', f'{self.spiderfoot_path}/sf.py',
                '-s', target,
                '-o', 'json'
            ]
            
            self.logger.info(f"Running SpiderFoot on target: {target}")
            result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=self.timeout)
            
            if result.returncode != 0:
                self.logger.error(f"SpiderFoot failed: {result.stderr}")
                return {'findings': [], 'error': result.stderr}
            
            # Parse JSON output
            findings = json.loads(result.stdout) if result.stdout else []
            
            # Extract entities
            entities = self._extract_entities(findings)
            relationships = self._extract_relationships(findings)
            
            return {
                'findings': findings,
                'entities': entities,
                'relationships': relationships,
                'count': len(findings)
            }
        
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"SpiderFoot execution failed: {str(e)}")
            return {'error': str(e), 'findings': []}
    
    def _extract_entities(self, findings):
        entities = set()
        for finding in findings:
            if isinstance(finding, dict):
                entity = finding.get('entity')
                if entity:
                    entities.add(entity)
        return list(entities)
    
    def _extract_relationships(self, findings):
        relationships = []
        for finding in findings:
            if isinstance(finding, dict) and 'entity' in finding:
                relationships.append({
                    'source': finding.get('source'),
                    'target': finding.get('entity'),
                    'relationship_type': finding.get('type')
                })
        return relationships
```

```python
class NucleiTool(BaseModule):
    """Nuclei - Fast and customizable vulnerability scanner with YAML templates"""
    
    def execute(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        target = input_data.get('target')
        templates = input_data.get('templates', 'cves')
        
        cmd = ['nuclei', '-u', target, '-t', templates, '-json']
        
        result = subprocess.run(cmd, capture_output=True, text=True, timeout=self.timeout)
        
        vulnerabilities = []
        if result.stdout:
            for line in result.stdout.split('\n'):
                if line:
                    try:
                        vuln = json.loads(line)
                        vulnerabilities.append(vuln)
                    except:
                        pass
        
        return {'vulnerabilities': vulnerabilities, 'count': len(vulnerabilities)}
```

```python
class MetasploitTool(BaseModule):
    """Metasploit Framework - Exploit development and execution"""
    
    def execute(self, input_data: Dict[str, Any]) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        exploit_id = input_data.get('exploit')
        target = input_data.get('target')
        
        msfcmd = f"""
        use {exploit_id}
        set RHOSTS {target}
        run
        """
        
        # Execute via msfconsole or msfvenom
        result = subprocess.run(
            ['msfconsole', '-x', msfcmd],
            capture_output=True,
            text=True,
            timeout=self.timeout
        )
        
        return {'output': result.stdout, 'status': 'executed'}
```

### Pipeline 1: Complete Reconnaissance Pipeline (pipelines_v3/reconnaissance_pipeline.yaml)

```yaml
version: '3.0'
name: reconnaissance_pipeline
description: >
  Comprehensive reconnaissance pipeline combining passive OSINT, active scanning,
  subdomain enumeration, and network mapping. Designed for both breadth and depth
  of target discovery.

stages:
  - name: passive_osint
    description: Passive information gathering from public sources
    parallel: true
    continue_on_error: true
    timeout: 3600
    tools:
      - spiderfoot
      - censys
      - shodan
      - virustotal
      - urlhaus
    fallback_tools:
      - whois
      - dig
    transformations:
      - normalize_domains
      - deduplicate_ips
  
  - name: subdomain_enumeration
    description: Active and passive subdomain discovery
    parallel: true
    continue_on_error: true
    timeout: 1800
    tools:
      - amass
      - subfinder
      - sublist3r
      - knockpy
      - dnsdumpster
    fallback_tools:
      - crt_sh
      - dnsrecon

  - name: web_discovery
    description: Web crawling and endpoint discovery
    parallel: true
    continue_on_error: true
    timeout: 3600
    tools:
      - photon
      - katana
      - waybackfinder
      - httpx
    fallback_tools:
      - curl
      - wget

  - name: network_mapping
    description: Network service and port enumeration
    parallel: false
    continue_on_error: true
    timeout: 3600
    tools:
      - nmap
      - naabu
      - masscan
    fallback_tools:
      - zmap

  - name: technology_fingerprinting
    description: Identify technologies and frameworks
    parallel: true
    continue_on_error: true
    timeout: 1800
    tools:
      - wappalyzer
      - builtwith
      - whatcms

  - name: certificate_analysis
    description: SSL/TLS certificate enumeration
    parallel: true
    continue_on_error: true
    timeout: 1800
    tools:
      - ssl_scan
      - certstream
      - crt_sh

  - name: data_aggregation
    description: Consolidate and deduplicate findings
    parallel: false
    continue_on_error: false
    timeout: 600
    tools:
      - data_normalizer
      - relationship_extractor

outputs:
  - name: targets_json
    format: json
    path: /output/targets.json
  - name: relationships_json
    format: json
    path: /output/relationships.json
  - name: summary_report
    format: html
    path: /output/reconnaissance_report.html
```

```yaml
framework:
  name: r4ng3r-v3
  version: 3.0.0
  environment: production

logging:
  level: INFO
  format: json
  output:
    - file: /var/log/r4ng3r/framework.log
    - console: true
    - syslog: true

database:
  postgresql:
    host: localhost
    port: 5432
    database: r4ng3r_assets
    username: r4ng3r_user
    pool_size: 20
  
  mongodb:
    host: localhost
    port: 27017
    database: r4ng3r_results
    replica_set: rs0
  
  neo4j:
    host: localhost
    port: 7687
    database: neo4j
    auth_enabled: true

task_queue:
  broker: redis://localhost:6379
  backend: redis://localhost:6379
  workers: 10
  max_retries: 3
  timeout: 3600

api:
  host: 0.0.0.0
  port: 8000
  workers: 4
  timeout: 300
  enable_docs: true
  cors_origins:
    - http://localhost:3000
    - https://dashboard.example.com

tools:
  api_keys_file: /etc/r4ng3r/api_keys.secure
  tools_path: ./tools_v3
  auto_discover: true
  registry_cache_path: /tmp/r4ng3r_registry.json

limits:
  max_concurrent_tools: 10
  max_pipeline_stages: 50
  max_execution_time: 86400
  max_memory_gb: 32

security:
  api_key_validation: true
  rate_limiting: true
  requests_per_minute: 100
  allow_list_enabled: false
```

SECTION 7: DEPLOYMENT GUIDE
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

### 7.1: Quick Start (Docker)

```bash
# Clone the repository
git clone https://github.com/oscarwangr-creator/R4nger-v2.git
cd R4nger-v2

# Build Docker image
docker build -t r4ng3r-v3:latest .

# Run with Docker Compose
docker-compose up -d

# Access API
curl http://localhost:8000/api/health

# Access Dashboard
open http://localhost:3000
```

### 7.2: Manual Installation

```bash
# Install Python dependencies
pip install -r requirements.txt

# Install system tools
bash scripts/install_tools.sh

# Configure API keys
cp config/api_keys.yaml.example config/api_keys.yaml
# Edit with your API keys

# Initialize databases
python scripts/init_databases.py

# Start framework
python -m r4ng3r.main --config config/framework_config.yaml
```

### 7.3: Kubernetes Deployment

```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: r4ng3r-v3
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: r4ng3r
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: r4ng3r
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: r4ng3r
        image: r4ng3r-v3:latest
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8000
        env:
        - name: DATABASE_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: r4ng3r-secrets
              key: database-url
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
          limits:
            memory: "4Gi"
            cpu: "2000m"
```

```
GET    /api/executions                - List executions
GET    /api/executions/{execution_id} - Get execution details
POST   /api/workflows/{workflow}/run  - Execute workflow
```

SECTION 9: COMPLETE USAGE EXAMPLES

### Example 1: Execute Reconnaissance Pipeline

```python
from r4ng3r.core_v3 import PipelineEngine, ToolRegistry

# Initialize
registry = ToolRegistry()
registry.auto_discover_tools()

engine = PipelineEngine(registry)

# Execute reconnaissance pipeline
result = engine.execute_pipeline(
    'reconnaissance_pipeline',
    {
        'domain': 'example.com',
        'passive_only': False
    }
)

print(f"Found {len(result['relationships'])} relationships")
print(f"Execution time: {result['duration']}")
```

### Example 2: Execute Full Pentest Workflow

```python
from r4ng3r.core_v3 import WorkflowEngine

workflow_engine = WorkflowEngine()

result = workflow_engine.execute_workflow(
    'full_pentest_workflow',
    {
        'target': 'example.com',
        'scope': ['*.example.com'],
        'aggressive': True
    }
)
```

### Example 3: Custom Tool Execution

```python
from r4ng3r.tools_v3.reconnaissance import AmassTool

tool = AmassTool({
    'name': 'amass',
    'mode': 'active',
    'api_keys': {
        'shodan': 'YOUR_KEY'
    }
})

result = tool.run({
    'domain': 'example.com'
})
```

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 10: TROUBLESHOOTING & OPTIMIZATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

### Common Issues & Solutions

1. **Tool not found in registry**
   - Verify tool file is in tools_v3/ directory
   - Check file naming convention: `{tool_name}_tool.py`
   - Ensure class inherits from BaseModule
   - Run auto_discover_tools() after adding tools

2. **Pipeline execution timeout**
   - Increase timeout in pipeline YAML
   - Reduce parallel workers
   - Check system resources
   - Review tool-specific timeouts

3. **Database connection errors**
   - Verify database services are running
   - Check connection credentials
   - Review firewall rules
   - Check database reachability

4. **API key authentication failures**
   - Verify API keys in config
   - Check key permissions/scopes
   - Review rate limiting
   - Check key expiration

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 11: PERFORMANCE OPTIMIZATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

### Optimization Strategies

1. **Parallel Execution**
   - Set parallel: true in pipeline stages
   - Adjust max_concurrent_tools in config
   - Monitor system resources

2. **Caching**
   - Enable result caching for repeated queries
   - Configure cache TTL
   - Use Redis for distributed caching

3. **Rate Limiting**
   - Implement exponential backoff
   - Respect API rate limits
   - Queue long-running tasks

4. **Database Indexing**
   - Create indexes on frequently queried fields
   - Optimize query patterns
   - Archive old results

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
SECTION 12: SECURITY CONSIDERATIONS
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

### Best Practices

1. **API Key Management**
   - Store keys in secure vault (HashiCorp Vault)
   - Rotate keys regularly
   - Use service accounts
   - Implement principle of least privilege

2. **Network Security**
   - Use VPN/proxy for outbound connections
   - Implement firewall rules
   - Separate tool execution environments
   - Use TLS for all communications

3. **Data Protection**
   - Encrypt sensitive data at rest
   - Use secure channels (HTTPS, SSH)
   - Implement access controls
   - Audit all access

4. **Tool Isolation**
   - Run tools in containers
   - Use resource limits
   - Implement sandboxing
   - Monitor tool behavior

R4nger-V3 COMPLETE FRAMEWORK UPGRADE DOCUMENT
EXECUTIVE SUMMARY
This document outlines the transformation of R4nger-V2 into R4nger-V3, an enterprise-grade autonomous penetration testing and OSINT platform with:

500+ integrated tools across 15+ domains
Distributed execution with master-worker architecture
Intelligent feedback loops for autonomous targeting
AI-optional modules that enhance but don't require LLM integration
Fault-tolerant pipelines that continue despite tool failures
Commercial/military-grade security and reporting
SECTION 1: CURRENT STATE ANALYSIS
R4nger-V2 Strengths:

Modular architecture foundation
YAML-based pipeline definitions
Basic tool integration patterns
CLI and API interfaces
Reporting engine (HTML/PDF/JSON)
Critical Gaps:

No distributed execution framework
Limited tool coverage (23 modules vs. 500+)
Static pipeline definitions
No autonomous intelligence loops
Weak error handling in multi-tool scenarios
Limited OSINT automation

SECTION 3: ADVANCED PIPELINE ARCHITECTURES
Pipeline 1: COMPLETE OSINT INTELLIGENCE LOOP
YAML
pipeline: complete_osint_loop
version: "3.0"
description: "Autonomous multi-stage OSINT with intelligent feedback"

inputs:
  target: "email|username|domain|phone|person_name"
  
stages:
  - name: "Phase 1 - Initial Reconnaissance"
    parallel: true
    tools:
      - name: "sherlock_username_search"
        input_key: "username"
        fallback_chain: ["maigret", "namechk", "beenjammin"]
        continue_on_error: true
        output_mapping: "social_media_profiles"
        
      - name: "theHarvester_email_enum"
        input_key: "domain"
        fallback_chain: ["simplyemail", "emailfinder"]
        continue_on_error: true
        output_mapping: "discovered_emails"
        
      - name: "amass_subdomain_enum"
        input_key: "domain"
        config:
          passive_sources: ["all"]
          active_scan: false
        fallback_chain: ["subfinder", "sublist3r"]

Python
class IntelligenceFeedbackLoop:
    """
    Autonomous intelligence gathering and expansion system.
    Continuously refines targets and triggers new pipelines based on discoveries.
    """
    
    def __init__(self, database, pipeline_engine, ai_module=None):
        self.db = database
        self.pipeline_engine = pipeline_engine
        self.ai_module = ai_module
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        
    def analyze_results(self, pipeline_results):
        """
        Analyze pipeline results to identify:
        1. New target pivots
        2. High-value targets
        3. Exploitation opportunities
        4. Intelligence gaps requiring additional recon
        """
        analysis = {
            'new_targets': [],
            'pivots': [],
            'opportunities': [],
            'follow_up_tasks': []
        }
        
        # Extract all discovered entities
        entities = self._extract_entities(pipeline_results)
        
        # Correlate with existing intelligence
        correlations = self._correlate_with_existing(entities)
        
        # Identify new pivots
        for correlation in correlations:
            if correlation['confidence'] > 0.7:
                analysis['pivots'].append(correlation)
                
        # AI-based analysis for prioritization
        if self.ai_module:
            analysis['opportunities'] = self.ai_module.rank_opportunities(entities)
        else:
            analysis['opportunities'] = self._rule_based_ranking(entities)
            
        return analysis
        
    def trigger_new_pipelines(self, analysis):
        """Auto-trigger new reconnaissance pipelines based on discoveries"""
        for pivot in analysis['pivots']:
            new_target = pivot['target']
            pipeline_name = self._determine_best_pipeline(pivot['type'])
            
            self.logger.info(f"Auto-triggering {pipeline_name} for {new_target}")
            self.pipeline_engine.queue_pipeline(pipeline_name, {'target': new_target})
            
    def _extract_entities(self, results):
        """Extract all entities from pipeline results"""
        entities = {
            'emails': set(),
            'domains': set(),
            'ips': set(),
            'usernames': set(),
            'phone_numbers': set(),
            'credentials': [],
            'services': [],
            'vulnerabilities': []
        }
        
        # Implementation extracts data from results
        # ...
        
        return entities
        
    def _determine_best_pipeline(self, entity_type):
        """Select most appropriate pipeline for entity type"""
        pipeline_map = {
            'email': 'complete_osint_loop',
            'domain': 'domain_intelligence_pipeline',
            'ip': 'infrastructure_reconnaissance',
            'username': 'identity_intelligence_loop',
            'phone': 'phone_intelligence_pipeline'
        }
        return pipeline_map.get(entity_type, 'complete_osint_loop')

Amass Integration Module
Python
import subprocess
import json
import asyncio
from typing import List, Dict, Any
from core_v2.base_tool import BaseTool

class AmassIntegration(BaseTool):
    """
    OWASP Amass - Enterprise asset discovery and DNS enumeration
    """
    
    name = "amass"
    description = "Subdomain enumeration, DNS reconnaissance, and network asset discovery"
    version = "4.2.0"
    categories = ["reconnaissance", "dns_enumeration", "asset_discovery"]
    
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        super().__init__(config)
        self.amass_path = config.get('amass_path', '/usr/bin/amass')
        self.api_keys = config.get('api_keys', {})
        self.passive_mode = config.get('passive_mode', True)
        
    def validate_input(self) -> bool:
        """Validate that Amass is installed and config is correct"""
        try:
            result = subprocess.run([self.amass_path, 'enum', '-h'], 
                                  capture_output=True, timeout=10)
            return result.returncode == 0
        except:
            return False
            
    def execute(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Execute Amass enumeration"""
        domain = self.args.get('target')
        if not domain:
            return {'status': 'error', 'message': 'No target domain provided'}
            
        try:
            # Prepare Amass configuration
            amass_config = self._build_amass_config()
            
            # Run passive enumeration
            if self.passive_mode:
                passive_results = self._run_passive_enum(domain, amass_config)
            else:
                passive_results = {}
                
            # Run active enumeration if enabled
            active_results = {}
            if self.args.get('active_scan', False):
                active_results = self._run_active_enum(domain, amass_config)
                
            # Merge and deduplicate results
            all_subdomains = set()
            all_subdomains.update(passive_results.get('subdomains', []))
            all_subdomains.update(active_results.get('subdomains', []))
            
            # Build comprehensive output
            output = {
                'status': 'success',
                'target': domain,
                'subdomains': list(all_subdomains),
                'dns_records': self._extract_dns_data(passive_results),
                'infrastructure': self._analyze_infrastructure(all_subdomains),
                'netblocks': passive_results.get('netblocks', []),
                'asset_count': len(all_subdomains)
            }
            
            # Save to database
            self.save_to_database(output)
            
            return output
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Amass execution failed: {str(e)}")
            return {'status': 'error', 'message': str(e)}
            
    def _run_passive_enum(self, domain: str, config: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Execute Amass passive enumeration"""
        cmd = [
            self.amass_path, 'enum',
            '-d', domain,
            '-passive',
            '-json', '-o', '/tmp/amass_passive.json'
        ]
        
        # Add data sources if configured
        if config.get('data_sources'):
            cmd.extend(['-src', ','.join(config['data_sources'])])
            
        try:
            subprocess.run(cmd, timeout=3600, check=True)
            with open('/tmp/amass_passive.json', 'r') as f:
                results = json.load(f)
            return self._parse_amass_output(results)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Passive enum failed: {str(e)}")
            return {}
            
    def _run_active_enum(self, domain: str, config: Dict) -> Dict:
        """Execute Amass active enumeration with brute forcing"""
        cmd = [
            self.amass_path, 'enum',
            '-d', domain,
            '-brute',
            '-o', '/tmp/amass_active.json',
            '-json'
        ]
        
        try:
            subprocess.run(cmd, timeout=7200, check=True)
            with open('/tmp/amass_active.json', 'r') as f:
                results = json.load(f)
            return self._parse_amass_output(results)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Active enum failed: {str(e)}")
            return {}
            
    def _parse_amass_output(self, amass_json: List[Dict]) -> Dict:
        """Parse Amass JSON output into structured format"""
        subdomains = set()
        ips = set()
        netblocks = []
        dns_records = []
        
        for entry in amass_json:
            if entry.get('Type') == 'FQDN':
                subdomains.add(entry.get('Name'))
            elif entry.get('Type') == 'IPAddress':
                ips.add(entry.get('Address'))
            elif entry.get('Type') == 'Netblock':
                netblocks.append(entry.get('CIDR'))
            elif entry.get('Type') == 'DNS':
                dns_records.append(entry)
                
        return {
            'subdomains': list(subdomains),
            'ips': list(ips),
            'netblocks': netblocks,
            'dns_records': dns_records
        }
        
    def _build_amass_config(self) -> Dict:
        """Build Amass configuration with API keys"""
        config = {}
        
        # Add API keys if available
        if self.api_keys.get('shodan'):
            config['shodan_key'] = self.api_keys['shodan']
        if self.api_keys.get('virustotal'):
            config['vt_key'] = self.api_keys['virustotal']
        if self.api_keys.get('securitytrails'):
            config['st_key'] = self.api_keys['securitytrails']
            
        return config

class AutonomousIntelligenceLoop:
    """
    Self-expanding OSINT system that autonomously identifies and investigates new targets
    """
    def __init__(self):
        self.knowledge_base = {}
        self.pipeline_queue = []
        self.discovered_entities = set()
        
    def process_pipeline_result(self, result):
        """Extract entities and auto-trigger new investigations"""
        # Example: Found email bob@acme.com → trigger email breach check → trigger domain enum
        new_entities = self.extract_entities(result)
        
        for entity in new_entities:
            if entity not in self.discovered_entities:
                self.discovered_entities.add(entity)
                # Auto-determine best pipeline
                next_pipeline = self.select_pipeline(entity)
                self.pipeline_queue.append((next_pipeline, entity))
                
    def extract_entities(self, result):
        """Extract: emails, domains, IPs, usernames, phones, companies"""
        entities = {
            'emails': self._extract_emails(result),
            'domains': self._extract_domains(result),
            'ips': self._extract_ips(result),
            'usernames': self._extract_usernames(result),
            'phones': self._extract_phones(result)
        }
        return self._flatten_entities(entities)
        
    def select_pipeline(self, entity):
        """
        Intelligently select which pipeline to run next
        - Found email → run email_intel_pipeline
        - Found domain → run domain_enum_pipeline
        - Found company → run company_assessment_pipeline
        """
        entity_type = self.classify_entity(entity)
        pipeline_map = {
            'email': 'email_intelligence_pipeline',
            'domain': 'domain_enumeration_pipeline',
            'ip': 'infrastructure_reconnaissance',
            'username': 'identity_intelligence_loop',
            'phone': 'phone_intelligence_pipeline',
            'company': 'company_osint_pipeline'
        }
        return pipeline_map.get(entity_type, 'complete_osint_loop')

3. INTELLIGENT TOOL FALLBACK SYSTEM

Python
class ToolFallbackChain:
    """
    If tool fails, automatically try backup tools without stopping pipeline
    """
    PRIMARY_TOOLS = {
        'subdomain_enum': [
            'amass',           # Primary
            'subfinder',       # Fallback 1
            'sublist3r',       # Fallback 2
            'assetfinder'      # Fallback 3
        ],
        'port_scan': [
            'nmap',            # Primary (comprehensive but slow)
            'naabu',           # Fallback 1 (fast alternative)
            'masscan',         # Fallback 2 (very fast)
            'zmap'             # Fallback 3 (raw socket fast)
        ],
        'web_scan': [
            'nuclei',          # Primary (template-based)
            'nikto',           # Fallback 1 (CGI scanning)
            'wappalyzer',      # Fallback 2 (tech detection)
            'whatweb'          # Fallback 3 (basic scan)
        ]
    }
    
    def execute_with_fallback(self, tool_category, target):
        """Try primary tool, fall back if it fails"""
        chain = self.PRIMARY_TOOLS[tool_category]
        
        for tool in chain:
            try:
                result = self.run_tool(tool, target)
                if result and result.get('status') == 'success':
                    return {'tool': tool, 'data': result, 'status': 'success'}
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.warning(f"{tool} failed: {e}, trying next...")
                continue
                
        # All tools failed - log but continue pipeline
        return {'status': 'all_fallbacks_failed', 'category': tool_category}
Pipeline Impact: ✓ Continues with partial data if tools fail

Python
class AdaptivePipelineEngine:
    def execute(self, pipeline_name, target):
        """Execute pipeline with adaptive branching"""
        result = {}
        
        # Stage 1: Initial reconnaissance
        recon_results = self.run_stage('reconnaissance', target)
        
        # Stage 2: Analyze and determine next pipeline
        discovered_services = recon_results['services']
        next_pipeline = self.determine_next_pipeline(discovered_services)
        
        # Stage 3: Execute selected pipeline
        exploitation_results = self.run_pipeline(next_pipeline, target)
        
        return exploitation_results
        
    def determine_next_pipeline(self, services):
        """Select exploitation pipeline based on discovered services"""
        pipeline_map = {
            'wordpress': 'wordpress_exploitation',
            'joomla': 'joomla_exploitation',
            'drupal': 'drupal_exploitation',
            'apache_struts': 'struts_cve_pipeline',
            'jenkins': 'jenkins_pipeline',
            'tomcat': 'tomcat_pipeline'
        }
        for service in services:
            if service in pipeline_map:
                return pipeline_map[service]
        return 'generic_web_exploitation'

class GraphIntelligenceLayer:
    """
    Store all discovered data as Neo4j graph for relationship discovery
    """
    def __init__(self):
        self.graph = Neo4jConnection()
        
    def ingest_osint_results(self, results):
        """Add all entities as nodes and relationships"""
        # Create nodes
        for email in results['emails']:
            self.graph.create_node('Email', {'address': email})
            
        for domain in results['domains']:
            self.graph.create_node('Domain', {'name': domain})
            
        for ip in results['ips']:
            self.graph.create_node('IP', {'address': ip})
            
        # Create relationships
        for breach in results['breaches']:
            email = breach['email']
            password_hash = breach['password']
            self.graph.create_relationship(
                ('Email', email),
                'FOUND_IN_BREACH',
                ('Breach', breach['name']),
                {'password_hash': password_hash}
            )
            
    def discover_relationships(self, query):
        """
        Example: "Find all people connected to John Doe"
        Returns: All emails, domains, companies, phone numbers connected to John
        """
        return self.graph.cypher(query)
        
    def example_queries(self):
        queries = {
            'find_connected_accounts': """
                MATCH (person:Person)-[*1..3]-(account:Email)
                WHERE person.name = 'John Doe'
                RETURN account
            """,
            'find_company_infrastructure': """
                MATCH (company:Company)-[:OWNS]->(domain:Domain)
                       -[:HAS_SUBDOMAIN]->(subdomain:Domain)
                       -[:RESOLVES_TO]->(ip:IP)
                WHERE company.name = 'Target Corp'
                RETURN ip
            """,
            'breach_correlation': """
                MATCH (email:Email)-[:FOUND_IN]->(breach1:Breach),
                      (email)-[:FOUND_IN]->(breach2:Breach)
                WHERE breach1 <> breach2
                RETURN email, collect(breach1.name + ', ' + breach2.name)
            """
        }
        return queries
Benefit: Identify hidden connections and relationships between discovered entities

7. OPTIONAL AI/LLM ENHANCEMENT LAYER
Impact: 8% - Intelligent decision making (doesn't break if unavailable)

Key Principle: AI is optional, not required

Python
class OptionalAIEnhancement:
    """
    AI assists but system works perfectly without it
    """
    def __init__(self, ai_enabled=False):
        self.ai_enabled = ai_enabled
        if ai_enabled:
            self.llm = OpenAIClient()  # or Claude, or local Llama
            
    def rank_vulnerabilities(self, vulns):
        """Rank vulnerabilities by exploitability"""
        if self.ai_enabled:
            # Use AI for intelligent ranking
            prompt = f"Rank these vulns by exploitability: {vulns}"
            return self.llm.query(prompt)
        else:
            # Fall back to rule-based ranking
            return self.rule_based_ranking(vulns)
            
    def generate_report_summary(self, findings):
        """Generate executive summary"""
        if self.ai_enabled:
            return self.llm.generate_summary(findings)
        else:
            return self.template_based_summary(findings)
            
    def suggest_next_action(self, current_status):
        """AI suggests what to test next"""
        if self.ai_enabled:
            return self.llm.suggest_next_steps(current_status)
        else:
            return self.heuristic_suggestions(current_status)

8. COMPREHENSIVE ERROR RESILIENCE & LOGGING
Impact: 8% - Prevents cascading failures

Current State: Tool fails → unclear error Upgrade: Detailed error recovery and intelligent retries

Python
class ResilientExecution:
    """
    Execute with comprehensive error handling and recovery
    """
    MAX_RETRIES = 3
    RETRY_DELAYS = [5, 15, 60]  # Exponential backoff
    
    def execute_tool_with_resilience(self, tool_name, args):
        """Execute with retry logic and detailed logging"""
        for attempt in range(self.MAX_RETRIES):
            try:
                # Attempt execution
                result = self.execute_tool(tool_name, args)
                
                if result['status'] == 'success':
                    self.log_success(tool_name, result)
                    return result
                    
            except ToolTimeout as e:
                self.log_error(f"Tool timeout: {tool_name}", e)
                if attempt < self.MAX_RETRIES - 1:
                    wait_time = self.RETRY_DELAYS[attempt]
                    self.logger.info(f"Retrying {tool_name} in {wait_time}s...")
                    time.sleep(wait_time)
                    
            except DependencyMissing as e:
                self.log_error(f"Tool not installed: {tool_name}", e)
                return {'status': 'tool_missing', 'tool': tool_name}
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.log_error(f"Unexpected error in {tool_name}", e)
                if attempt >= self.MAX_RETRIES - 1:
                    return {'status': 'failed', 'error': str(e)}
                    
        return {'status': 'failed_after_retries', 'attempts': self.MAX_RETRIES}

5.3 Tool Integration Template (BaseTool Pattern)
All 500 tools inherit from this pattern:

Python
class BaseTool:
    """
    Template for all tool integrations
    Every tool in R4nger-V3 inherits from this
    """
    
    # Required metadata
    name = "tool_name"
    description = "Tool description"
    version = "1.0"
    categories = ["category1", "category2"]
    input_schema = {
        'type': 'object',
        'properties': {
            'target': {'type': 'string'},
            'options': {'type': 'object'}
        },
        'required': ['target']
    }
    output_schema = {
        'type': 'object',
        'properties': {
            'status': {'type': 'string'},
            'results': {'type': 'array'}
        }
    }
    
    def __init__(self, config: Dict[str, Any]):
        self.config = config
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(self.name)
        
    def validate_input(self) -> bool:
        """Check if tool is available and input is valid"""
        raise NotImplementedError
        
    def execute(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Execute the tool"""
        raise NotImplementedError
        
    def parse_output(self, raw_output) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """Convert tool output to standard format"""
        raise NotImplementedError
        
    def save_to_database(self, results):
        """Store results in central database"""
        # Implemented in base class
        pass
        
    def normalize_output(self, results) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """
        Normalize output to standard schema:
        {
            'status': 'success|error',
            'tool': 'tool_name',
            'timestamp': ISO8601,
            'target': 'target_info',
            'results': [...],
            'errors': [...],
            'metadata': {...}
        }
        """
        return {
            'status': 'success',
            'tool': self.name,
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
            'results': results
        }
SECTION 6: ADVANCED PIPELINE ARCHITECTURE
6.1 Pipeline Execution Model
R4nger-V3 pipelines support:

Sequential Execution - Tools run one after another
Parallel Execution - Multiple tools run simultaneously
Conditional Branching - Different paths based on results
Feedback Loops - Results trigger new pipelines
Error Recovery - Fallback tools on failure
Timeout Management - Tool execution time limits
Resource Throttling - CPU/Memory/Network limits
Progress Tracking - Real-time status updates
Result Aggregation - Combine multi-tool outputs
Graph Integration - Automatic relationship mapping
6.2 Complete OSINT Intelligence Loop Pipeline
This is the most sophisticated pipeline in V3:

YAML
pipeline: "autonomous_osint_intelligence_loop"
version: "3.0"
description: "Self-expanding OSINT with relationship discovery and autonomous pivoting"
category: "osint"
difficulty: "advanced"
estimated_duration: "12-24 hours (fully autonomous)"

# Input validation
input_validation:
  target_types: ["email", "username", "domain", "phone", "person_name", "company"]
  min_depth: 1
  max_depth: 5  # Prevent infinite loops

# Global configuration
global_config:
  parallel_workers: 5
  timeout_per_tool: 600  # 10 minutes
  max_retries: 3
  retry_delay: [5, 15, 60]  # Exponential backoff
  continue_on_error: true
  save_intermediate_results: true
  graph_ingestion: true
  
# Stage 1: Initial Target Analysis
stages:
  - stage_id: 1
    name: "Initial Target Classification & Expansion"
    description: "Classify target and begin initial reconnaissance"
    parallel: false
    
    tasks:
      - task_id: 1.1
        name: "Target Classification"
        tool: "target_classifier"
        input:
          target: "${input.target}"
        operation: "classify_and_expand"
        outputs:
          - "target_type"
          - "expanded_targets"  # e.g., domain → subdomains
        
      - task_id: 1.2
        name: "Historical Intelligence"
        tool: "history_searcher"
        input_depends_on: "1.1"
        input:
          target: "${stages.1.tasks.1.1.outputs.expanded_targets[0]}"
        operation: "search_historical_data"
        outputs:
          - "historical_breaches"
          - "previous_findings"
          - "known_vulnerabilities"

# Stage 2: Multi-Source OSINT Gathering (Parallel)
  - stage_id: 2
    name: "Multi-Source OSINT Gathering"
    description: "Parallel reconnaissance from all available sources"
    parallel: true
    depends_on: [1]
    
    parallel_config:
      max_workers: 8
      timeout: 1800  # 30 minutes total
      
    tasks:
      - task_id: 2.1
        name: "Social Media Discovery"
        parallel_subtasks:
          - tool: "sherlock"
            input: "target"
            timeout: 300
            
          - tool: "maigret"
            input: "target"
            timeout: 300
            fallback_to: "sherlock"
            
          - tool: "namecheck"
            input: "target"
            timeout: 180
            
        aggregation: "merge_deduplicate"
        outputs:
          - "social_profiles"
          
      - task_id: 2.2
        name: "Email Discovery"
        parallel_subtasks:
          - tool: "theHarvester"
            input: "${stages.1.tasks.1.1.outputs.expanded_targets}"
            timeout: 600
            
          - tool: "hunter_io"
            input: "domain"
            api_key: "${env:HUNTER_IO_API_KEY}"
            timeout: 60
            
          - tool: "clearbit"
            input: "domain"
            api_key: "${env:CLEARBIT_API_KEY}"
            timeout: 60
            fallback_to: "theHarvester"
            
          - tool: "simplyemail"
            input: "target"
            timeout: 300
            
        aggregation: "merge_deduplicate_validate"
        outputs:
          - "discovered_emails"
          - "company_emails"
          - "personal_emails"
          
      - task_id: 2.3
        name: "Subdomain & DNS Reconnaissance"
        parallel_subtasks:
          - tool: "amass"
            input:
              domain: "${stages.1.tasks.1.1.outputs.expanded_targets[0]}"
              mode: "passive"
            timeout: 900
            config:
              data_sources: ["all_passive"]
              
          - tool: "subfinder"
            input:
              domain: "${stages.1.tasks.1.1.outputs.expanded_targets[0]}"
            timeout: 600
            fallback_to: "assetfinder"
            
          - tool: "crtsh"
            input:
              domain: "${stages.1.tasks.1.1.outputs.expanded_targets[0]}"
            timeout: 180
            
          - tool: "certstream"
            input:
              domain: "${stages.1.tasks.1.1.outputs.expanded_targets[0]}"
            timeout: 300
            
        aggregation: "merge_deduplicate"
        outputs:
          - "subdomains"
          - "certificates"
          
      - task_id: 2.4
        name: "Breach Database Checking"
        parallel_subtasks:
          - tool: "haveibeenpwned"
            input:
              targets: "${stages.2.tasks.2.2.outputs.discovered_emails}"
            timeout: 60
            api_key: "${env:HIBP_API_KEY}"
            
          - tool: "dehashed"
            input:
              query: "${stages.2.tasks.2.2.outputs.discovered_emails}"
            timeout: 120
            api_key: "${env:DEHASHED_API_KEY}"
            
          - tool: "leakdb"
            input:
              targets: "${stages.2.tasks.2.2.outputs.discovered_emails}"
            timeout: 60
            
        aggregation: "merge_rank_by_confidence"
        outputs:
          - "breach_data"
          - "leaked_passwords"
          - "leaked_hashes"

# Stage 3: Relationship Mapping & Correlation
  - stage_id: 3
    name: "Intelligent Correlation & Analysis"
    description: "Correlate all discovered data and identify relationships"
    parallel: false
    depends_on: [2]
    
    tasks:
      - task_id: 3.1
        name: "Data Correlation"
        operation: "intelligent_correlation"
        input:
          social_profiles: "${stages.2.tasks.2.1.outputs.social_profiles}"
          emails: "${stages.2.tasks.2.2.outputs.discovered_emails}"
          subdomains: "${stages.2.tasks.2.3.outputs.subdomains}"
          breaches: "${stages.2.tasks.2.4.outputs.breach_data}"
        ai_enhanced: true
        ai_model: "claude_correlation"
        fallback_logic: "rule_based_correlator"
        outputs:
          - "correlated_entities"
          - "relationship_graph"
          - "confidence_scores"
          
      - task_id: 3.2
        name: "New Target Detection"
        operation: "autonomous_pivot_detection"
        input_depends_on: "3.1"
        logic:
          # Example pivot rules:
          # email@company.com → company.com (domain pivot)
          # john.doe@company.com → "John Doe" (person pivot)
          # subdomain.company.com → company.com (infrastructure pivot)
          
        outputs:
          - "new_targets_identified"
          - "pivot_type"
          - "confidence_level"

# Stage 4: Threat Intelligence Integration
  - stage_id: 4
    name: "Threat Intelligence Analysis"

# Stage 5: Autonomous Expansion
  - stage_id: 5
    name: "Autonomous Expansion"
    description: "Automatically trigger follow-up investigations on new targets"
    parallel: false
    depends_on: [3]
    conditional: true

      - if: "pivot_count > 0"
        then: "trigger_recursive_investigation"

# Stage 6: Comprehensive Report Generation
  - stage_id: 6
    name: "Intelligence Report Generation"
    description: "Generate multi-format report with findings"
    parallel: false
    depends_on: [3, 4, 5]
    
    tasks:

        name: "Report Generation"
        operation: "generate_comprehensive_report"

        include:

          - relationship_diagram
          - timeline
          - recommendations
        ai_summary: true
        
# Error handling
error_handling:
  strategy: "continue_with_next_tool"
  on_tool_failure:
    action: "try_fallback"
    max_fallbacks: 3
    log_all_attempts: true
    
  on_stage_failure:
    action: "log_and_continue"
    notify_operator: true
    
# Output specification
outputs:
  primary:
    - "comprehensive_osint_report.html"
    - "correlated_intelligence.json"
    - "relationship_graph.neo4j"
    
  secondary:
    - "timeline.json"
    - "threat_assessment.pdf"
    - "recommendations.txt"

  on_completion: "final_report_email"
